<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sestien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sestēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sestien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sehstehun</i>. ***zestig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zestig.html>zestig</a> (5118)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sestich</i>, also <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsestich</i> with <i>t-</i> from <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsēventich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sestig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sehs tigiwiz</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zestig.html>zestig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>sixty</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">z-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/s/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>z-</i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to the former prefix <i>t-</i> (see etymology). However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/z/</span> in line with the spelling.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>

***zeta.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeta.html>zeta</a> (25500)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From the <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ζῆτα</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">zêta</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeta.html>zeta</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">zetas</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>The sixth letter of the modern Greek alphabet (<i class="Grek mention" lang="el">Ζ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">Z</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">ζ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">z</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) preceded by <a href = vnd.unilang:epsilon.html>epsilon</a> (<i class="Grek mention" lang="el">Ε</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">E</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">ε</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">e</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>) and followed by eta, (<i class="Grek mention" lang="el">Η</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">I</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="Grek mention" lang="el">η</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="el-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">i</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>); or the seventh letter in the ancient Greek alphabet, in which it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> preceded by digamma (<i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">Ϝ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">W</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ϝ</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">w</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>)</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mathematical function formally known as the Riemann <a href = vnd.unilang:zeta.html>zeta</a> function.
<dl><dd><i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zeta.html>Zeta</a></b> of 3 <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> irrational</i></dd></dl></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">setel</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*setal</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*<a href = vnd.unilang:setl.html>setl</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*setlaz</i>. ***zetten.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zetten.html>zetten</a> (577)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">setten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">setten</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*satjaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sodéyeti</i>, causative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to sit</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>

***zeug.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>zeug</a> (20894)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">soge</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">suege</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*soga</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sugō</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*suh₂kéh₂</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sū-</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Söög</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">sûch</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sow</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">sugga</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="no">sugge</i>. The regular form in Middle Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">soge</i> with a back vowel, with fronted <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">suege</i> occurring only in the western dialects. The original form <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> still found dialectally as <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zoog.html>zoog</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>zeug</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeugen.html>zeugen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>zeugje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>sow (female pig)
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonyms:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:keu.html>keu</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:mot.html>mot</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">figuratively<span class="ib-comma">,</span> derogatory</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:bitch.html>bitch</a>, cow, blatant term of abuse for a 'beastly' human female</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zeug.html>zeug</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">v</span> <sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><span style="background-color:FFFFE0;font-style: italic;">(<a href = vnd.unilang:veeteelt.html>veeteelt</a>)</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrouwelijk.html>vrouwelijk</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:varken.html>varken</a></li>

***zeven.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a> (766)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēven</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sivun</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sivon</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebun</i>, from earlier <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebunt</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*septḿ̥</i>, with <i>-t</i> added through influence of "nine" and "ten".
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>seven</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēven</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeef.html>zeef</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>

</p>
<ol><li>to sift, sieve, strain

***zevende.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zevende.html>zevende</a> (5129)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēvende</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sivondo</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebundô</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zevende.html>zevende</a></strong> (<i>not comparable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>seventh</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zevenentwintig.html>zevenentwintig</a> (25070)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeven.html>zeven</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:twintig.html>twintig</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zevenentwintig.html>zevenentwintig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>twenty-seven</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Hoofdtelwoord"><i>Hoofdtelwoord</i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zevenentwintig.html>zevenentwintig</a></b>

***zeventien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeventien.html>zeventien</a> (5090)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seventien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sivontēn</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sivontien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebuntehun</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">seventeen</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">santjin</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">siebzehn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">sytten</i>.
</p>

***zeventig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a> (10010)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sēventich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sivontig</i>, but also Middle Dutch <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">tsēventich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*antsivontig</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sebuntēhundą</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Numeral">Numeral</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeventig.html>zeventig</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>seventy</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Although <a href = vnd.unilang:spelt.html>spelt</a> with <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">z-</i>, the word <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> traditionally pronounced with initial <span class="IPA">/s/</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> in accents that generally do not devoice <i>z-</i>. This <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> due to the former prefix <i>t-</i> (see etymology). However, there are also many <a href = vnd.unilang:speakers.html>speakers</a> who pronounce <span class="IPA">/z/</span> in line with the spelling.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zeveren.html>zeveren</a> (37535)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sêveren</i>. </p>

***zich.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> (176)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">sich</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">sih</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*<a href = vnd.unilang:sik.html>sik</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sek</i>. Old Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> not have a reflexive pronoun (only rarely in early Limburgish texts), but used the normal accusative pronoun (if necessary intensified by <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">selven</i>, cf. English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">himself</i>). Although the use of <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></i> in Holland-based Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> clearly triggered by written German, this development <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> assisted by the fact that the south-eastern dialects of Dutch <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> already adopted certain High German pronoun forms in much earlier times (cf. Limburgish <i class="Latn mention" lang="li">ich</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="li"><a href = vnd.unilang:mich.html>mich</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="li"><a href = vnd.unilang:dich.html>dich</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="li"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></i>).
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_2">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Third person singular and plural reflexive pronoun</span>; himself, herself, itself, themselves, oneself
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wast.html>wast</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b>.</i>  |  He washes <b>himself</b>.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wast.html>wast</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gezicht.html>gezicht</a>.</i>  |  He washes his face.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ieder.html>Ieder</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:voor.html>voor</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b>.</i>  |  Every <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> for <b>himself</b>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">by extension<span class="ib-comma">,</span> formal<span class="ib-comma">,</span> reflexive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Second person singular and plural formal reflexive pronoun</span>; yourself, yourselves
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sloeg.html>Sloeg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> in <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:donker.html>donker</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>Did</a> you hit <b>yourself</b> in the dark?</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>U</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kunt.html>kunt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:scheren.html>scheren</a>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">You can shave here.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:vergist.html>Vergist</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a>?</i> ― <span class="e-translation"><a href = vnd.unilang:aren.html>Aren</a>'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you mistaken?</span></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="use-with-mention">expresses an unintended result with many otherwise non-reflexive and ergative verbs</span>
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:viel.html>viel</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ongeluk.html>ongeluk</a></i>  |  He fell and this resulted in an accident.</dd>
<dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lachte.html>lachte</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bult.html>bult</a></i>  |  He laughed so severely that it left him a hunchback.</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>Zich</a></i> can be used whether the reflexivity of the verb <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> optional or mandatory. Optionally reflexive verbs can also take <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zichzelf.html>zichzelf</a></i> as reflexive pronoun.</li>
<li>As in English (but unlike German and French), Dutch reflexive pronouns do not express reciprocity, except dialectally. Reciprocal senses may occur in fixed verb constructions, as in: <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></i> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:verloofd.html>verloofd</a></i>. (“They have got engaged.”) Such <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a> are generally explainable by etymology. (In the example, the original sense <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> “They have promised themselves [to each other].”)</li></ul>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame" style="float: left; width: 65em">

</div></div>

***zichtbaar.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zichtbaar.html>zichtbaar</a> (6637)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">sichtbar</i>, equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zicht.html>zicht</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-baar</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

***zichzelf.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zichzelf.html>zichzelf</a> (675)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Univerbation of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zelf.html>zelf</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zichzelf.html>zichzelf</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>oneself; himself/herself/themselves</li>
<li>yourself (in combination with the polite pronoun <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>.)</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zichzelf.html>Zichzelf</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> primarily used with verbs that are <i>optionally</i> reflexive. Verbs with mandatory reflexivity like <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vergissen.html>vergissen</a></i> typically take <a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a>. Exceptions to this strong tendency show up, however, though this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a marginal but not per se erroneous phenomenon. Hendriks, Spenader and Smits (2008) note in a corpus 638 occurrences of the mandatorily reflexive verb <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ontpoppen.html>ontpoppen</a></i> involving the reflexive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zich.html>zich</a></i>, versus 1 with the reflexive <i><a href = vnd.unilang:zichzelf.html>zichzelf</a></i>.</li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">siekebedde</i>. ***ziel.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziel.html>ziel</a> (930)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">siele</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sēla</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sēola</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*siola</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*saiwalō</i>. Compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">Seel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">siel</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Seele</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">soul</i>.
</p>

***zien.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a> (94)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sien</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:sian.html>sian</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sehwaną</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*sekʷ-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to see, notice</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally a class 5 strong verb, but the Germanic <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*h</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lost.html>lost</a> from the infinitive and present tense forms through syncope in Old Dutch. However, it alternated with <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*g</i> in the past tense through <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Grammatischer_Wechsel" class="extiw" title="w:Grammatischer Wechsel">Grammatischer Wechsel</a>, and this remained.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to see
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zie.html>zie</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jouw.html>jouw</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:kat.html>kat</a>!</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>see</b> your cat!</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Werkwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:werkwoord.html>Werkwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zien.html>zien</a></b>
</p>

***zier.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zier.html>zier</a> (18502)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:sieren.html>siere</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Frankish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Frankish language">Frankish</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*seuro</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-West_Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-West Germanic language">Proto-West Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gmw-pro">*seur(j)ōn</i>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> borrowed into French as <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr">ciron</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">itch-mite</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. The ultimate origin <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> unknown, as cognates outside of West Germanic are lacking.  Perhaps ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kes-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scrape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, source of <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Ancient_Greek" class="extiw" title="w:Ancient Greek">Ancient Greek</a></span> <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ξύω</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">xúō</span>, <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to scratch, scrape</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>

</p>
<ol><li>A tiny amount.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A mite.</li></ol>

<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:zigeuner.html>Zigeuner</a></i>. See the German entry for further etymological information.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zigeuner.html>zigeuner</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zigeuners.html>zigeuners</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zigeuner.html>zigeunertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>, <i>feminine</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zigeunerin.html>zigeunerin</a></b>)

<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Gypsy, member of the Roma</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">sometimes offensive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> gypsy, person who leads a nomadic life</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes_2">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>Sometimes considered offensive by Romani people. Use of the word for Non-Romani people may also be considered offensive, and may also be considered incorrect.

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijde.html>zijde</a> (2938)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">side</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sīda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīdǭ</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijde.html>zijde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijden.html>zijden</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>side, face <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">of an object</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:kant.html>kant</a></span></span></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">side</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*sīda</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">saeta</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijde.html>zijde</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="feminine gender">f</abbr></span> (<i>uncountable</i>)
</p>
<ol><li>silk</li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_3">Etymology 3</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sidi</i>, a contraction of <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sijt gi</i> (modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijt.html>zijt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>).
</p>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<p>The contraction <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> sometimes reinforced with an additional <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>, giving <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijde.html>zijde</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gij.html>gij</a></i>.

***zijn.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> (20)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sīn</i>. The infinitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i> along with the <a href = vnd.unilang:words.html>words</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a></i> (present indicative and subjunctive) derive ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₁es-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> no separate infinitive in Germanic. The modern infinitive <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> probably back-formed in late Old Dutch from the first-person plural subjunctive <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sīn</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:we.html>we</a> be</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, since this form <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> become identical to the infinitive in other verbs during the late Old Dutch period. Compare also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sein.html>sein</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Low_German" class="extiw" title="w:Low German">Low German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds">sien</i>.
</p><p>The original infinitive survives in <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wesen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wesan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wesaną</i>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂wes-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to reside</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. All the forms with initial <i>w-</i> (imperative and past tense) derive from this root.
</p><p>Finally, the forms <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a></i> derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*beuną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to be, to become</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*BʰuH-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to become</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, which survives only as relic forms in the West Germanic languages and not at all in the others. Its infinitive and non-singular forms are only attested in (Old) English.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To be, to exist.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a></b> of <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vraag.html>vraag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">To <b>be</b> or not to <b>be</b>, that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> the question.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>Was</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afgelopen.html>afgelopen</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zaterdag.html>zaterdag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ook.html>ook</a>?</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation"><b><a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>Were</a></b> you there too last Saturday?</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> copulative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to connect a noun to an adjective that describes it.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bal.html>bal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:rond.html>rond</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The ball <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> round.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense of the active voice of some verbs, together with a past participle.<br /><b>Note:</b> The <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense of most other verbs <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using <a href = vnd.unilang:hebben.html>hebben</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hier.html>hier</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:geweest.html>geweest</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">He <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a> here.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> tense of the passive voice, together with a past participle.<br /><b>Note:</b> The imperfect tense passive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> formed using <a href = vnd.unilang:worden.html>worden</a>.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ze.html>Ze</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:gered.html>gered</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">They <b><a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:saved.html>saved</a>.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschilderd.html>geschilderd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The wall <b><a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> painted.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:muur.html>muur</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zal.html>zal</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:geschilderd.html>geschilderd</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The wall will <b>have <a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> painted.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> auxiliary</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to form the continuous forms of various tenses, together with <b><a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a></b> or, in archaic style, with a present participle.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:aan.html>aan</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:lopen.html>lopen</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">The <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></b> walking.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To go, to go on a trip and return.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dokter.html>dokter</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I <b>am going</b> to the doctor for a while.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ben.html>ben</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naar.html>naar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:strand.html>strand</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:geweest.html>geweest</a>.</b></i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">I've <b><a href = vnd.unilang:been.html>been</a></b> to the beach today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> impersonal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="use-with-mention">Used to indicate weather, temperature or some other general condition.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:erg.html>erg</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vandaag.html>vandaag</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">It <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> very <a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a> today.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> copulative<span class="ib-comma">,</span> mathematics</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to be, to equal, to total, to amount to; <span class="use-with-mention">used to indicate that the values on either side of an equation are the same.</span>
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:drie.html>Drie</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:keer.html>keer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijf.html>vijf</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vijftien.html>vijftien</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">Three times five <b><a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a></b> fifteen.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Inflection">Inflection</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li>Generally, the infinitive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></i>, the present participle <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">wezend</i> and the present subjunctive <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weze.html>weze</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></i> are also used. While the subjunctive <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> considered archaic, it persists in some fixed expressions such as <i><a href = vnd.unilang:als.html>als</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ware.html>ware</a></i> ("as if [it] <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a>").</li>
<li><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>Zijn</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:has.html>has</a> special forms for the pronominal imperatives of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a></i> and <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a></i>. Thus, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weest.html>weest</a></i> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>!</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></i> <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a>!</i>, rather than the regular <i><a href = vnd.unilang:bent.html>bent</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:u.html>u</a>!, <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:jullie.html>jullie</a>!</i>, which are less common. The simple imperative <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wees.html>wees</a></i> in all <a href = vnd.unilang:cases.html>cases</a>. In Belgium the singular imperative <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zij.html>zij</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> also used.</li></ul>

<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">archaic in standard Dutch</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wezen.html>wezen</a></span></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete in standard Dutch</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">bennen</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sijn</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sīn</i> (originally a reflexive form), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīnaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*seyno-</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:sein.html>sein</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">sin</i>. Ultimately a form of the Proto-Indo-European reflexive pronoun <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*swe</i>, related to Russian <i class="Cyrl mention" lang="ru">себя</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="ru-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">sebja</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, Latin <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">suus</i>, Ancient Greek <i class="polytonic mention" lang="grc">ἑός</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span lang="grc-Latn" class="mention-tr tr Latn">heós</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> etc.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></strong> (<i>dependent possessive, independent possessive</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b>, <i>contracted form</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">z'n</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>Third-person singular, masculine and neuter possessive pronoun: his, its.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hond.html>hond</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> and <b>his</b> dog.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b>z'n</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:hoed.html>hoed</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>man</a> and <b>his</b> hat.</span></dd></dl></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>Een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:boek.html>boek</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:en.html>en</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kaft.html>kaft</a>.</i><dl><dd><span class="e-translation">A book and <b>its</b> cover.</span></dd></dl></div></dd></dl></li></ol>

***zijne.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a> (2608)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sine</i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">non-attributive form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></span> (English: his)
<dl><dd>Normally used in conjunction with the definite article <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a>, depending on the gender of what <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> being referred to.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>Die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:auto.html>auto</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That car <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b> one. <i>or</i> That car <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That house <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b> one. <i>or</i> That house <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b>.</span></div></dd>
<dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a>/<a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b>.</i> ― <span class="e-translation">That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b> one. <i>or</i> That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b>his</b>.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">archaic or dialectal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> <span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Inflected form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></i></span></span>
<dl><dd>Used for plurals in archaic literary style.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrienden.html>vrienden</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i>contemporary Dutch:</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:vrienden.html>vrienden</a>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></i> ― <span class="e-translation">These are <b>his</b> friends.</span></div></dd></dl></dd>
<dd>Used for masculine singulars in Flemish and Brabantian dialects.
<dl><dd><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijne.html>zijne</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a>. <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content"><i>standard Dutch:</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:stoel.html>stoel</a>.</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></i> ― <span class="e-translation">That's <b>his</b> chair.</span></div></dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
